How to use this Timetable

How to Use this Timetable
This timetable is designed so you can determine United flight information easily
and conveniently. The guide below will show you how to read this timetable.

Disclaimer
Data shown is for information only. Schedules are subject to change without notice.
The miles shown are MileagePlus frequent flyer mileage, and the information is provided
as a convenience to MileagePlus members. Actual flown miles will be posted to your account.
Fare class, MileagePlus Premier status bonuses and other promotional bonuses are not 
included in the totalslisted. A minimum of 500 MileagePlus miles is earned for flights less than
500 miles in distance. For AMTRAK train segments 250 MileagePlus miles is awarded for Economy
Class and 325 MileagePlus miles for First Class.

Constructing Your Own Connection
This timetable highlights information about United's non-stop and select
direct flight schedule.
To organize your connecting flight(s), follow the instructions below.
* Choose a flight from your origin city to a connection city on the most direct
  route to your destination.
* Note arrival time at connection city.
* Minimum connecting times vary between airports. Please allow at least 45
  minutes for a domestic connection and at least 90 minutes for an international connection.
* Locate a flight to your final destination.
* Example: To connect from Miami, FL (MIA) to Los Angeles CA (LAX) you could
  choose flight 1891 departing Miami at 6:25A and
  arriving in Houston at 8:04A Your connecting flight 1495,
  departs Houston at 9:15A and arrives in Los Angeles at 10:42A
